NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
(Under Section 72 of Partnership Act 1932.)
It is hereby notified that the registered partnership firm by name “SUPREME WEAVING MILLS, ERODE” registered as
Regn. No. 291/2005 of Registrar of firm, Erode District, being a partnership at will was dissolved with effect from 18-6-2015
on the issuance of a notice of dissolution by its partner N. MANOHARAN, son of Thiru P.M. Nachimuthu, residing
at 15/4, Uzhavan Nagar, Surampatti Post, Erode-638 009.
Erode,
30th October 2015.

N. MANOHARAN.

FORM NO. 155.
(See Rule 329)
Members Winding Up
SOUTHERN LPG LIMITED.
No. 2, (OLD No. 33), VENUGOPAL AVENUE, CHETPET, CHENNAI-600 031.
NOTICE CONVENING FINAL MEETING.
Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 that a General Meeting of the Members of the above named
Company will be held on Friday, the 11th day of December 2015, at the Registered Office at No. 2, (Old No. 33). Venugopal
Avenue, Chetpet, Chennai-600 031 at 11.00 a.m. for the purpose of having an account laid before the members showing
them the manner in which the winding up has been conducted and the property of the company disposed of and of hearing
any explanation that may be given by the liquidator and also of determining by a special resolution of the company, the
manner in which the books, accounts and documents of the company and of the liquidator shall be disposed of.
Dated this the 4th day of November, 2015.
Chennai,
30th October 2015.

S. BABU.
Liquidator.
